add_namespace = ottoman

country_event = { #ottoman revolt
	id = ottoman.0
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		random_controlled_state = {
			limit = { resistance > 79.9 }
			controller = { set_temp_variable = { global.occupier_country = THIS } }
			set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_state = THIS }
			if = {
				limit = { has_resistance = yes }
				set_resistance = 0
			}
#			every_neighbor_state = {
#				limit = {
#					controller = { tag = var:global.occupier_country }
#					is_core_of = var:global.occupier_country
#				}
#				add_resistance = 10
#			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					check_variable = { TUR_albanian_state_level > 0 }
					is_core_of = ALB
				}
				NOT = { country_exists = ALB }
			}
			ALB = {
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					check_variable = { TUR_albanian_state_level > 0 }
					is_core_of = ALB
				}
				country_exists = ALB
				ALB = { NOT = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country } }
			}
			create_dynamic_country = {
				original_tag = ALB
				copy_tag = ALB
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_neutrality = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_democratic = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_fascism = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_communism = 1 }
				# do not change ideology of occupier country
				var:global.occupier_country = {
					remove_from_allowed_party = yes
				}
				if = {
					# if occupied country exists and different than new country
					# it is white peaced & subject of occupier. ignore its ideology as well
					limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = global.occupied_country } } }
					var:global.occupied_country = {
						remove_from_allowed_party = yes
					}
				}
				# change government if necesarry
				random_list = {
					allowed_party_democratic = {
						set_popularities = {
							democratic = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = democratic elections_allowed = yes }
					}
					allowed_party_fascism = {
						set_popularities = {
							fascism = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism elections_allowed = no }
					}
					allowed_party_communism = {
						set_popularities = {
							communism = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = communism elections_allowed = no }
					}
					allowed_party_neutrality = {
						set_popularities = {
							neutrality = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					check_variable = { TUR_albanian_state_level > 0 }
					is_core_of = ALB
				}
				any_country_with_original_tag = {
					original_tag_to_check = ALB
					has_war_with = global.occupier_country
				}
			}
			random_country_with_original_tag = {
				original_tag_to_check = ALB
				limit = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country }
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					check_variable = { TUR_greek_state_level > 0 }
					is_core_of = IKR
				}
				NOT = { country_exists = IKR }
			}
			IKR = {
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = GRE_greek_resistance
					days = 365
				}
				add_ideas = standing_alone
				if = {
					limit = { GRE = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country } }
					GRE = {
						IKR = { get_current_government_type = yes }
						set_autonomy = {
							target = IKR
							autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_unilateral_union
						}
						IKR = {
							restore_previous_government_type = yes
							remove_ideas = standing_alone
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					check_variable = { TUR_greek_state_level > 0 }
					is_core_of = SMS
				}
				NOT = { country_exists = SMS }
			}
			SMS = {
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					check_variable = { TUR_greek_state_level > 0 }
					is_core_of = GRE
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = SMS
						is_core_of = IKR
						is_core_of = ALB
					}
				}
				NOT = { country_exists = GRE }
			}
			GRE = {
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					check_variable = { TUR_greek_state_level > 0 }
					is_core_of = GRE
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = SMS
						is_core_of = IKR
						is_core_of = ALB
					}
				}
				country_exists = GRE
				GRE = { NOT = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country } }
			}
			create_dynamic_country = {
				original_tag = GRE
				copy_tag = GRE
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_neutrality = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_democratic = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_fascism = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_communism = 1 }
				# do not change ideology of occupier country
				var:global.occupier_country = {
					remove_from_allowed_party = yes
				}
				if = {
					# if occupied country exists and different than new country
					# it is white peaced & subject of occupier. ignore its ideology as well
					limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = global.occupied_country } } }
					var:global.occupied_country = {
						remove_from_allowed_party = yes
					}
				}
				# change government if necesarry
				random_list = {
					allowed_party_democratic = {
						set_popularities = {
							democratic = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = democratic elections_allowed = yes }
					}
					allowed_party_fascism = {
						set_popularities = {
							fascism = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism elections_allowed = no }
					}
					allowed_party_communism = {
						set_popularities = {
							communism = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = communism elections_allowed = no }
					}
					allowed_party_neutrality = {
						set_popularities = {
							neutrality = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					check_variable = { TUR_greek_state_level > 0 }
					is_core_of = GRE
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = SMS
						is_core_of = IKR
						is_core_of = ALB
					}
				}
				any_country_with_original_tag = {
					original_tag_to_check = GRE
					has_war_with = global.occupier_country
				}
			}
			random_country_with_original_tag = {

						set_popularities = {
							fascism = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism elections_allowed = no }
					}
					allowed_party_communism = {
						set_popularities = {
							communism = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = communism elections_allowed = no }
					}
					allowed_party_neutrality = {
						set_popularities = {
							neutrality = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					check_variable = { TUR_assyrian_state_level > 0 }
					is_core_of = ASY
				}
				any_country_with_original_tag = {
					original_tag_to_check = ASY
					has_war_with = global.occupier_country
				}
			}
			random_country_with_original_tag = {
				original_tag_to_check = ASY
				limit = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country }
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					check_variable = { TUR_kurdish_state_level > 0 }
					is_core_of = KUR
				}
				NOT = { country_exists = KUR }
			}
			KUR = {
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					check_variable = { TUR_kurdish_state_level > 0 }
					is_core_of = KUR
				}
				country_exists = KUR
				KUR = { NOT = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country } }
			}
			create_dynamic_country = {
				original_tag = KUR
				copy_tag = KUR
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_neutrality = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_democratic = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_fascism = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_communism = 1 }
				# do not change ideology of occupier country
				var:global.occupier_country = {
					remove_from_allowed_party = yes
				}
				if = {
					# if occupied country exists and different than new country
					# it is white peaced & subject of occupier. ignore its ideology as well
					limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = global.occupied_country } } }
					var:global.occupied_country = {
						remove_from_allowed_party = yes
					}
				}
				# change government if necesarry
				random_list = {
					allowed_party_democratic = {
						set_popularities = {
							democratic = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = democratic elections_allowed = yes }
					}
					allowed_party_fascism = {
						set_popularities = {
							fascism = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism elections_allowed = no }
					}
					allowed_party_communism = {
						set_popularities = {
							communism = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = communism elections_allowed = no }
					}
					allowed_party_neutrality = {
						set_popularities = {
							neutrality = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					check_variable = { TUR_kurdish_state_level > 0 }
					is_core_of = KUR
				}
				any_country_with_original_tag = {
					original_tag_to_check = KUR
					has_war_with = global.occupier_country
				}
			}
			random_country_with_original_tag = {
				original_tag_to_check = KUR
				limit = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country }
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					check_variable = { TUR_romanian_state_level > 0 }
					is_core_of = ROM
				}
				NOT = { country_exists = ROM }
			}
			ROM = {
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					check_variable = { TUR_romanian_state_level > 0 }
					is_core_of = ROM
				}
				country_exists = ROM
				ROM = { NOT = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country } }
			}
			create_dynamic_country = {
				original_tag = ROM
				copy_tag = ROM
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_neutrality = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_democratic = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_fascism = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_communism = 1 }
				# do not change ideology of occupier country
				var:global.occupier_country = {
					remove_from_allowed_party = yes
				}
				if = {
					# if occupied country exists and different than new country
					# it is white peaced & subject of occupier. ignore its ideology as well
					limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = global.occupied_country } } }
					var:global.occupied_country = {
						remove_from_allowed_party = yes
					}
				}
				# change government if necesarry
				random_list = {
					allowed_party_democratic = {
						set_popularities = {
							democratic = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = democratic elections_allowed = yes }
					}
					allowed_party_fascism = {
						set_popularities = {
							fascism = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism elections_allowed = no }
					}
					allowed_party_communism = {
						set_popularities = {
							communism = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = communism elections_allowed = no }
					}
					allowed_party_neutrality = {
						set_popularities = {
							neutrality = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					check_variable = { TUR_romanian_state_level > 0 }
					is_core_of = ROM
				}
				any_country_with_original_tag = {
					original_tag_to_check = ROM
					has_war_with = global.occupier_country
				}
			}
			random_country_with_original_tag = {
				original_tag_to_check = ROM
				limit = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country }
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					check_variable = { TUR_georgian_state_level > 0 }
					is_core_of = GEO
				}
				NOT = { country_exists = GEO }
			}
			GEO = {
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					check_variable = { TUR_georgian_state_level > 0 }
					is_core_of = GEO
				}
				country_exists = GEO
				GEO = { NOT = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country } }
			}
			create_dynamic_country = {
				original_tag = GEO
				copy_tag = GEO
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_neutrality = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_democratic = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_fascism = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_communism = 1 }
				# do not change ideology of occupier country
				var:global.occupier_country = {
					remove_from_allowed_party = yes
				}
				if = {
					# if occupied country exists and different than new country
					# it is white peaced & subject of occupier. ignore its ideology as well
					limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = global.occupied_country } } }
					var:global.occupied_country = {
						remove_from_allowed_party = yes
					}
				}
				# change government if necesarry
				random_list = {
					allowed_party_democratic = {
						set_popularities = {
							democratic = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = democratic elections_allowed = yes }
					}
					allowed_party_fascism = {
						set_popularities = {
							fascism = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism elections_allowed = no }
					}
					allowed_party_communism = {
						set_popularities = {
							communism = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = communism elections_allowed = no }
					}
					allowed_party_neutrality = {
						set_popularities = {
							neutrality = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					check_variable = { TUR_georgian_state_level > 0 }
					is_core_of = GEO
				}
				any_country_with_original_tag = {
					original_tag_to_check = GEO
					has_war_with = global.occupier_country
				}
			}
			random_country_with_original_tag = {
				original_tag_to_check = GEO
				limit = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country }
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { TUR_armenian_state_level > 0 }
							is_core_of = ARM
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { TUR_greek_state_level > 0 }
							is_core_of = GRE
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_state_level > 0 }
							OR = {
								is_core_of = BUL
								is_core_of = SER
								is_core_of = MNT
							}
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { TUR_albanian_state_level > 0 }
							is_core_of = ALB
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { TUR_assyrian_state_level > 0 }
							is_core_of = ASY
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { TUR_romanian_state_level > 0 }
							is_core_of = ROM
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { TUR_georgian_state_level > 0 }
							is_core_of = GEO
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { TUR_kurdish_state_level > 0 }
							is_core_of = KUR
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { TUR_turkish_state_level > 0 }
							is_core_of = TUR
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { TUR_azerbaijani_state_level > 0 }
							is_core_of = AZR
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_possible_country = {
				random_select_amount = 1
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				limit = { var:global.occupied_state = { is_core_of = PREV } }
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { country_exists = var:global.occupied_country } }
					transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
					set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = var:global.occupied_country
						var:global.occupied_country = { has_war_with = var:global.occupier_country }
					}
					transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
					set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						any_country_with_original_tag = {
							original_tag_to_check = var:global.occupied_country
							NOT = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country }
						}
					}
					create_dynamic_country = {
						original_tag = var:global.occupied_country
						copy_tag = var:global.occupied_country
						transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
						set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
						set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_neutrality = 1 }
						set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_democratic = 1 }
						set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_fascism = 1 }
						set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_communism = 1 }
						# do not change ideology of occupier country
						var:global.occupier_country = {
							remove_from_allowed_party = yes
						}
						if = {
							# if occupied country exists and different than new country
							# it is white peaced & subject of occupier. ignore its ideology as well
							limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = global.occupied_country } } }
							var:global.occupied_country = {
								remove_from_allowed_party = yes
							}
						}
						# change government if necesarry
						random_list = {
							allowed_party_democratic = {
								set_popularities = {
									democratic = 100
								}
								set_politics = { ruling_party = democratic elections_allowed = yes }
							}
							allowed_party_fascism = {
								set_popularities = {
									fascism = 100
								}
								set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism elections_allowed = no }
							}
							allowed_party_communism = {
								set_popularities = {
									communism = 100
								}
								set_politics = { ruling_party = communism elections_allowed = no }
							}
							allowed_party_neutrality = {
								set_popularities = {
									neutrality = 100
								}
								set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		var:global.new_occupied_country = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = created_civil_war_template } }
				set_country_flag = created_civil_war_template
				division_template = {
					name = "Resistance"
					is_locked = yes
					regiments = {
						irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						irregular_infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
						irregular_infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
			clear_temp_array = checked_neighbours
			every_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					state = var:global.occupied_state
					impassable = no
				}
				# move our armies to back home
				teleport_armies = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_ally_with = global.occupier_country
							has_military_access_to = global.occupier_country
						}
					}
					to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
				}
				# create resistance units, number is relative to size of industry
				set_temp_variable = { num_units_to_create = building_level@arms_factory }
				add_to_temp_variable = { num_units_to_create = building_level@industrial_complex } 
				add_to_temp_variable = { num_units_to_create = 3 }
				clamp_temp_variable = { var = num_units_to_create min = 3 max = 6 }
				for_loop_effect = {
					end = num_units_to_create
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Resistance\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.7"
						owner = var:global.new_occupied_country
					}
				}
				# move our armies so they are not surrounded/create pockets
				every_neighbor_state = {
					limit = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = global.occupied_country
						is_core_of = global.occupied_country
						not = { is_in_array = { checked_neighbours = this } }
					}
					add_to_temp_array = { checked_neighbours = this }
					teleport_armies = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_ally_with = global.occupier_country
								has_military_access_to = global.occupier_country
							}
						}
						to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
					}
					set_state_province_controller = {
						controller = global.occupied_country
						limit = {
							is_ally_with = global.occupier_country
						}
					}
				}
			}
			# create war if necesarry
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country } }
				declare_war_on = { target = global.occupier_country type = annex_everything }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = ALB
						original_tag = MAC
					}
					has_war_with = global.occupier_country
				}
				var:global.occupier_country = { country_event = { id = ottoman.7 days = 2 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = ottoman.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_military_planning

	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ottoman.1.a
		retire_country_leader = yes
		promote_character = TUR_mehmed_said
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = TUR_mehmed_said
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democracy
				traits = { TUR_kucuk grand_vizier }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		TUR_increase_itilafist_power = yes
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
}

country_event = { #Elections of 1912
	id = ottoman.5
	title = ottoman.5.t
	desc = ottoman.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote
	trigger = {
		original_tag = TUR
		date > 1912.6.1
		date < 1913.1.1
		has_elections = yes
		NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_elections_1912 }
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = TUR_neutrality_party_long
				name = TUR_neutrality_party
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.5.a
		trigger = { has_war = no }
		TUR_mahmud_sevket = {
			promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
			promote_leader = yes
		}
		set_politics = {
		    ruling_party = neutrality
    	    election_frequency = 48
		    elections_allowed = yes
		}
		clr_country_flag = TUR_itilafist_regime
		set_country_flag = TUR_ittihadist_regime
		set_country_flag = TUR_elections_1912
		set_country_flag = TUR_ittihat_ve_terakki_victory_elections
		complete_national_focus = TUR_elections_of_1912
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				#code_ai_later
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.5.b
		trigger = { has_war = no }
		promote_character = TUR_mehmed_kamil
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = democratic
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		clr_country_flag = TUR_ittihadist_regime
		set_country_flag = TUR_itilafist_regime
		set_country_flag = TUR_elections_1912
		set_country_flag = TUR_hurriyet_ve_itilaf_victory_elections

country_event = { #ottomans ask french to join them russia ask ottomans dominion
	id = ottoman.26
	title = ottoman.26.t
	desc = ottoman.26.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ottoman.26.a
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = RUS
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			add_to_faction = TUR
		}
		remove_ideas = TUR_diplomatic_isolation_1
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = ottoman_democratic_party_value
				value = party_popularity@democratic
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = ottoman_neutrality_party_value
				value = party_popularity@neutrality
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = ottoman_communism_party_value
				value = party_popularity@communism
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = ottoman_fascism_party_value
				value = party_popularity@fascism
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				set_country_flag = ottomans_are_democratic
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				set_country_flag = ottomans_are_communist
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				set_country_flag = ottomans_are_neutrality
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				set_country_flag = ottomans_are_fascism
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_elections = yes
				}
				set_country_flag = ottomans_have_elections
			}
		}
		RUS = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = TUR
				autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion
				end_wars = yes
				end_civil_wars = no
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = ottoman_democratic_party_value
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = ottoman_neutrality_party_value
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = ottoman_communism_party_value
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = ottoman_fascism_party_value
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ottomans_are_democratic
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ottomans_are_communist
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ottomans_are_neutrality
					has_country_flag = ottomans_have_elections
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ottomans_are_neutrality
					NOT = { has_country_flag = ottomans_have_elections }
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ottomans_are_fascism
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_in_faction_with = RUS
							is_faction_leader = yes
						}
						tag = RUS
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ottoman.27 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.26.b
		hidden_effect = {
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_in_faction_with = RUS
							is_faction_leader = yes
						}
						tag = RUS
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ottoman.28 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #blockade of the eastern mediterranena
	id = ottoman.47
	title = ottoman.47.t
	desc = ottoman.47.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_destroyers
	trigger = {
		tag = TUR
		NOT = {
			has_autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_ottoman_committee_government
			enemies_naval_strength_ratio < 3
			has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade
		}
		any_enemy_country = {
			naval_strength_ratio = {
				tag = TUR
				ratio > 2
			}
			access_to_mediterranean = yes
		}
		check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade > 0 }
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade > 19 } }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_monthly_population = -0.2 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_consumer_goods_factor  = 0.1 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_war_stability_factor = -0.2 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade > 18 } }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_monthly_population = -0.19 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_consumer_goods_factor  = 0.095 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_war_stability_factor = -0.19 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade > 17 } }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_monthly_population = -0.18 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_consumer_goods_factor  = 0.09 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_war_stability_factor = -0.18 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade > 16 } }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_monthly_population = -0.17 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_consumer_goods_factor  = 0.085 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_war_stability_factor = -0.17 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade > 15 } }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_monthly_population = -0.16 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_consumer_goods_factor  = 0.08 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_war_stability_factor = -0.16 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade > 14 } }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_monthly_population = -0.15 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_consumer_goods_factor  = 0.075 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_war_stability_factor = -0.15 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade > 13 } }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_monthly_population = -0.14 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_consumer_goods_factor  = 0.07 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_war_stability_factor = -0.14 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade > 12 } }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_monthly_population = -0.13 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_consumer_goods_factor  = 0.065 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_war_stability_factor = -0.13 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade > 11 } }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_monthly_population = -0.12 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_consumer_goods_factor  = 0.06 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_war_stability_factor = -0.12 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade > 10 } }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_monthly_population = -0.11 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_consumer_goods_factor  = 0.055 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_war_stability_factor = -0.11 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade > 9 } }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_monthly_population = -0.1 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_consumer_goods_factor  = 0.05 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_war_stability_factor = -0.1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade > 8 } }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_monthly_population = -0.09 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_consumer_goods_factor  = 0.045 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_war_stability_factor = -0.09 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade > 7 } }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_monthly_population = -0.08 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_consumer_goods_factor  = 0.04 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_war_stability_factor = -0.080 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade > 6 } }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_monthly_population = -0.07 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_consumer_goods_factor  = 0.035 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_war_stability_factor = -0.07 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade > 5 } }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_monthly_population = -0.06 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_consumer_goods_factor  = 0.03 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_war_stability_factor = -0.06 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade > 4 } }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_monthly_population = -0.05 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_consumer_goods_factor  = 0.025 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_war_stability_factor = -0.05 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade > 3 } }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_monthly_population = -0.04 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_consumer_goods_factor  = 0.02 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_war_stability_factor = -0.04 }
			}
			else_if = {

				set_variable = { TUR_nb_monthly_population = -0.03 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_consumer_goods_factor  = 0.015 }
				set_variable = { TUR_nb_war_stability_factor = -0.03 }

			else_if = {

				set_variable = { TUR_nb_war_stability_factor = -0.02 }

				count = 1

					is_controlled_by = ROOT
					industrial_complex < 1
					arms_factory < 1

					TUR_state_has_minority = yes
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						industrial_complex > 1
						arms_factory > 1

					}
					TUR_state_has_minority = yes
				}
				set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_local_development_state_var = THIS }
			}
			country_event = ottoman.73
			clear_variable = ROOT.TUR_local_development_state_var
		}
		country_event = { id = ottoman.72 days = 180 random_days = 180 }
	}
}

					NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_frozen_foreign_assets_dm_foreign_power } }
				}
				ROOT = { add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_frozen_assets = PREV.opda_consumer_goods } }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_frozen_foreign_assets_dm_foreign_power }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.108.a
		add_ideas = TUR_frozen_foreign_assets
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
